RUS_voskhod_decisions = {
	RUS_increase_funding = {
		icon = GFX_decision_hol_attract_foreign_investors
		allowed = { always = no }
		visible = { has_country_flag = RUS_voskhod_active }
		cancel_if_not_visible = yes
		cost = 40
		days_remove = 14
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 10000
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = RUS_did_increase_funding_decision
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = RUS_republic_ai
					has_country_flag = RUS_empire_ai
					has_country_flag = RUS_socialist_ai
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision cancel RUS_increase_funding"
			hidden_effect = { add_political_power = 40 }
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision remove RUS_increase_funding"
			add_to_variable = { RUS_voskhod_cap = 50000 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_voskhod_remaining_mp = 50000 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_increase_voskhod_50000_tt
			RUS_check_voskhod_recruit = yes
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = yes }
				set_country_flag = RUS_did_increase_funding_decision
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}
	RUS_utilise_army = {
		icon = GFX_decision_soldierly_discipline
		allowed = { always = no }
		visible = { has_country_flag = RUS_voskhod_active }
		cancel_if_not_visible = yes
		days_remove = 20
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 10000
				has_country_flag = RUS_socialist_ai
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				check_variable = { RUS_military_anger < 2 }
				check_variable = { RUS_voskhod_cap < 160000 }
			}
		}
		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision cancel RUS_utilise_army"
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision remove RUS_utilise_army"
			add_to_variable = { RUS_voskhod_cap = 80000 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_voskhod_remaining_mp = 80000 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_increase_voskhod_80000_tt
			RUS_check_voskhod_recruit = yes
			set_temp_variable = { RUS_anger_change = 1 }
			RUS_change_military_anger = yes
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

	RUS_RASOLKO = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_merge_plant_materiel
		allowed = { always = no }
		visible = { has_country_flag = RUS_voskhod_active }
		cancel_if_not_visible = yes
		fire_only_once = yes
		custom_cost_text = RUS_rasolko_cost
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			NOT = { national_populist < 0.05 }
		}
		days_remove = 60
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 500
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = RUS_republic_ai
					has_country_flag = RUS_empire_ai
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = RUS_savinkov_ai
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision complete RUS_RASOLKO"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_popularity = { ideology = national_populist popularity = -0.05 }
			}
		}
		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision cancel RUS_RASOLKO"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_popularity = { ideology = national_populist popularity = 0.05 }
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision remove RUS_RASOLKO"
			add_to_variable = { RUS_voskhod_cap = 100000 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_voskhod_remaining_mp = 100000 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_increase_voskhod_100000_tt
			set_temp_variable = { RUS_anger_change = 1 }
			RUS_change_popular_anger = yes
			397 = { add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1 }
			213 = { add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1 }
			582 = { add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1 }
			568 = { add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1 }
			562 = { add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1 }
			409 = { add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1 }
			add_power_balance_value = {
				id = RUS_power_balance
				value = 0.05
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = russia_events.291 days = 95 } #Prisoner Labour
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

	RUS_norilsk_mining_and_metallurgy = {
		icon = steel
		allowed = { always = no }
		available = {
			custom_override_tooltip = {
				tooltip = { localization_key = has_completed_decision DECISION = RUS_far_north_construction_trust }
				has_country_flag = RUS_far_north_construction_trust_completed
			}
			#RUS_voskhod_check = yes
			check_variable = { RUS_voskhod_remaining_mp > 49999 }
			FROM = { is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT }
		}
		visible = { has_country_flag = RUS_voskhod_active }
		cancel_if_not_visible = yes
		custom_cost_text = RUS_voskhod_cost_50
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			NOT = { has_manpower < 50000 }
		}
		state_target = yes
		days_remove = 90
		fire_only_once = yes
		ai_will_do = { base = 80 }
		highlight_states = { highlight_state_targets = { state = 516 } } #Taymyr
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision complete RUS_norilsk_mining_and_metallurgy"
			hidden_effect = { add_manpower = -50000 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_voskhod_current_mp = 50000 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_voskhod_total_mp = 50000 }
			subtract_from_variable = { RUS_voskhod_remaining_mp = 50000 }
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision remove RUS_norilsk_mining_and_metallurgy"
			subtract_from_variable = { RUS_voskhod_current_mp = 50000 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_voskhod_remaining_mp = 50000 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_completed_voskhod_projects = 1 }
			RUS_check_voskhod_events = yes
			add_resource = {
				type = steel
				amount = 30
				state = 516
			}
			add_resource = {
				type = chromium
				amount = 24
				state = 516
			}
			RUS_decrease_black_monday = yes
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

	RUS_far_north_construction_trust = {
		icon = GFX_decision_cement_mixer
		allowed = { always = no }
		available = {
			#RUS_voskhod_check = yes
			check_variable = { RUS_voskhod_remaining_mp > 79999 }
			FROM = { is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT }
		}
		visible = { has_country_flag = RUS_voskhod_active }
		cancel_if_not_visible = yes
		custom_cost_text = RUS_voskhod_cost_80
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			NOT = { has_manpower < 80000 }
		}
		state_target = yes
		days_remove = 150
		fire_only_once = yes
		ai_will_do = { factor = 200 }
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 562 #Okhotsk
				state = 574 #Yakutsk
				state = 575 #Kirensk
				state = 637 #Kamchatka
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision complete RUS_far_north_construction_trust"
			hidden_effect = { add_manpower = -80000 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_voskhod_current_mp = 80000 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_voskhod_total_mp = 80000 }
			subtract_from_variable = { RUS_voskhod_remaining_mp = 80000 }
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision remove RUS_far_north_construction_trust"
			subtract_from_variable = { RUS_voskhod_current_mp = 80000 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_voskhod_remaining_mp = 80000 }
			set_country_flag = RUS_far_north_construction_trust_completed
			add_to_variable = { RUS_completed_voskhod_projects = 1 }
			RUS_check_voskhod_events = yes
			562 = { #Okhotsk
				add_building_construction = { type = infrastructure level = 1 }
			}
			574 = { #Yakutsk
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
				add_building_construction = { type = infrastructure level = 1 }
			}
			575 = { #Kirensk
				add_building_construction = { type = infrastructure level = 1 }
			}
			637 = { #Kamchatka
				add_building_construction = { type = infrastructure level = 1 }
			}
			add_resource = {
				type = steel
				amount = 10
				state = 644
			}
			RUS_decrease_black_monday = yes
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

RUS_the_great_patriotic_war_decisions = {
	RUS_barrier_troops = {
		priority = 21
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_police_action
		ai_will_do = { base = 5 }
		allowed = { always = no }
		available = {
			surrender_progress > 0.10
		}
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = RUS_desperate_measures
			any_enemy_country = { is_actual_major = yes }
		}
		days_remove = -1
		ai_hint_pp_cost = 50
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_CP_50_pp_50
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			NOT = { command_power < 50 }
			NOT = { has_political_power < 50 }
		}
		modifier = {
			army_org_regain = 0.15
			army_defence_factor = 0.1
			max_command_power = -40
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				surrender_progress < 0.01
				has_war = no
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision complete RUS_barrier_troops"
			add_stability = -0.03
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

	### Defense of Moscow ###
	RUS_hold_moscow = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_protection
		allowed = {
			always = no
		}
		#Fail trigger
		available = {
			NOT = { controls_state = 219 }
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 180
		fire_only_once = yes
		is_good = yes
		#Success
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision timeout RUS_hold_moscow"
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = RUS_relocated_capital_samara }
				add_war_support = 0.05
			}
			else = { add_war_support = 0.1 }
			add_war_support = 0.1
			clr_country_flag = RUS_battle_for_moscow_flag
		}
		#Fail
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision complete RUS_hold_moscow"
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = RUS_relocated_capital_samara }
				add_war_support = -0.05
			}
			else = {
				add_war_support = -0.1
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { RUS_savinkov = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { RUS_anger_change = 10 }
					RUS_change_military_anger = yes
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = RUS_battle_for_moscow_flag
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

	RUS_transfer_factories_to_the_urals = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_mountain_fortification
		available = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT }
					any_neighbor_state = {
						NOT = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
						owner = { has_war_with = ROOT }
					}
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_industrial_transfer_unlocked
			OR = {
				has_war_with = GER
				has_war_with = INT
			}
			FROM = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				OR = {
					arms_factory > 0
					industrial_complex > 0
				}
			}
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_war = no
				NOT = { controls_state = FROM }
			}
		}

		cost = RUS_industrial_transfer_cost?4
		days_remove = 15
		fire_only_once = no
		on_map_mode = map_only

		state_target = yes
		target_array = RUS_evacuation_states_array
		target_root_trigger = { has_country_flag = RUS_industrial_transfer_unlocked }
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				OR = {
					arms_factory > 0
					industrial_complex > 0
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 1000
				NOT = { has_full_control_of_state = FROM }
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision complete RUS_transfer_factories_to_the_urals"
			set_country_flag = RUS_has_evacuated_industry
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { RUS_industrial_transfer_cost < 100 } }
				add_to_variable = {
					RUS_industrial_transfer_cost = 4
					tooltip = RUS_industrial_transfer_cost
				}
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision remove RUS_transfer_factories_to_the_urals"
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { arms_factory > 0 } }
				FROM = {
					add_to_variable = { RUS_removed_arms_factory = 1 }
					remove_building = { type = arms_factory level = 1 }
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					prioritize = { 653 572 582 571 570 }
					limit = {
						is_siberia = yes
						is_core_of = ROOT
						free_building_slots = { building = arms_factory size > 1 include_locked = no }
					}
					add_to_variable = { RUS_added_arms_factory = 1 }
					add_building_construction = { type = arms_factory level = 1 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				FROM = {
					add_to_variable = { RUS_removed_industrial_complex = 1 }
					remove_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					prioritize = { 653 572 582 571 570 }
					limit = {
						is_siberia = yes
						is_core_of = ROOT
						free_building_slots = { building = industrial_complex size > 1 include_locked = no }
					}
					add_to_variable = { RUS_added_industrial_complex = 1 }
					add_building_construction = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}
	RUS_revert_the_industrial_transfer = {
		icon = fortress

		available = {
			has_war = no
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_has_evacuated_industry
		}

		cost = 50
		days_remove = 100
		fire_only_once = yes

		ai_will_do = { factor = 1000 }

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision complete RUS_revert_the_industrial_transfer"
			clr_country_flag = RUS_industrial_transfer_unlocked
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision remove RUS_revert_the_industrial_transfer"
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { has_variable = RUS_added_arms_factory }
				remove_building = { type = arms_factory level = var:RUS_added_arms_factory }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { has_variable = RUS_removed_arms_factory }
				add_building_construction = { type = arms_factory level = var:RUS_removed_arms_factory }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { has_variable = RUS_added_industrial_complex }
				remove_building = { type = industrial_complex level = var:RUS_added_industrial_complex }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { has_variable = RUS_removed_industrial_complex }
				add_building_construction = { type = industrial_complex level = var:RUS_removed_industrial_complex }
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

RUS_ongoing_election = {
	RUS_election_timer = {
		icon = GFX_decision_SWI_swiss_democratic_tradition_campaign
		allowed = { always = no } #manually activated
		available = { hidden_trigger = { always = no } }
		selectable_mission = yes
		is_good = no
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 90
		cancel_trigger = { has_socialist_government = yes }
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision timeout RUS_election_timer"
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { RUS_kadet_var < RUS_PSR_var } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { RUS_kadet_var < RUS_VPP_var } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { RUS_kadet_var < RUS_RDP_var } }
				}
				set_country_flag = RUS_kadet_victory
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { RUS_PSR_var < RUS_kadet_var } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { RUS_PSR_var < RUS_VPP_var } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { RUS_PSR_var < RUS_RDP_var } }
				}
				set_country_flag = RUS_PSR_victory
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { RUS_RDP_var < RUS_kadet_var } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { RUS_RDP_var < RUS_VPP_var } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { RUS_RDP_var < RUS_PSR_var } }
				}
				set_country_flag = RUS_RDP_victory
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = RUS_VPP_victory
			}
			country_event = russia_elections_events.30
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}
}

			hidden_effect = {
				remove_targeted_decision = { decision = RUS_pass_progressive_legislation target = ROOT }
				remove_targeted_decision = { decision = RUS_maklakov_resign target = ROOT }
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision complete RUS_political_apathy"

			hidden_effect = {
				remove_targeted_decision = { decision = RUS_pass_progressive_legislation target = ROOT }
				remove_targeted_decision = { decision = RUS_maklakov_resign target = ROOT }
			}
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision timeout RUS_political_apathy"
			clamp_variable = { var = RUS_apathy_var min = 0 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_apathy_tt
			add_to_variable = { RUS_apathy_var = 1 }
			set_temp_variable = { RUS_apathy_temp = RUS_apathy_var }
			divide_temp_variable = { RUS_apathy_temp = -100 }
			set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = RUS_apathy_temp }
			change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
			add_war_support = RUS_apathy_temp
			activate_mission = RUS_political_apathy
		}
	}

				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = RUS_strong_democracy
						has_idea = RUS_strenghtening_democracy
					}
				}
				RUS_decrease_democracy = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_active_mission = RUS_SVR_activity }
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = RUS_SVR_activity
					days = 60
				}
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { totalist > 0.05 }
				add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = -0.05 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					radical_socialist > 0.05
					is_in_coalition_with_radical_socialist = no
				}
				add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = -0.05 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					social_democrat > 0.1
					syndicalist < 0.05
					radical_socialist < 0.05
					totalist < 0.05
					is_part_of_government_social_democrat = no
				}
				add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = -0.05 }
			}
			else = { add_stability = 0.03 }
			set_temp_variable = { RUS_anger_change = -1 }
			RUS_change_right_anger = yes
			if = {
				limit = { has_active_mission = RUS_SVR_activity }
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = RUS_SVR_activity
					days = 60
				}
			}

		icon = GFX_decision_eng_trade_unions_support
		available = {
			OR = {

				has_decision = RUS_russia_is_monarchy

					check_variable = { RUS_marlib_var > 0 }
					check_variable = { RUS_soccon_var > 0 }
					check_variable = { RUS_mil_var > 0 }
				}
			}
			custom_override_tooltip = {
				tooltip = RUS_pass_constitution_2_tt
				check_variable = { RUS_mil_var > 0 }
			}
			custom_override_tooltip = {
				tooltip = RUS_pass_constitution_4_tt
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 6
					has_decision = RUS_russia_is_republic
					has_decision = RUS_russia_is_monarchy
					has_decision = RUS_confidence_votes
					has_decision = RUS_decrees
					has_decision = RUS_electoral_threshold

					has_decision = RUS_enshrine_military_role

			NOT = { has_decision = RUS_start_from_scratch }

					}

				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = RUS_democratic_foundation }

						remove_idea = RUS_democratic_foundation

						add_idea = RUS_russian_civil_society_3
					}

					add_days_mission_timeout = {
						mission = RUS_bold_promises
						days = 90
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { RUS_sorokin_var = 2 } }
				add_political_power = 150
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = RUS_democratic_foundation }
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = RUS_democratic_foundation
						add_idea = RUS_russian_civil_society_1
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_idea = RUS_democratic_foundation_2 }
					swap_ideas = {

					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_political_power = 125
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = RUS_democratic_foundation
					add_idea = RUS_russian_civil_society_1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = RUS_strong_democracy }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = RUS_strong_democracy
					add_idea = RUS_genuine_democracy
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = RUS_embers_of_democracy
						has_idea = RUS_weak_democracy
						has_idea = RUS_unstable_democracy
						has_idea = RUS_strenghtening_democracy
					}
				}
				RUS_increase_democracy = yes
			}
			else = { add_political_power = 100 }
			remove_targeted_decision = { decision = RUS_rural_schools_program target = ROOT }
			remove_targeted_decision = { decision = RUS_minority_representation target = ROOT }
			remove_targeted_decision = { decision = RUS_secular_campaign target = ROOT }
			remove_targeted_decision = { decision = RUS_sociological_institute target = ROOT }
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}
}

RUS_USNS_decision_cat = {
	RUS_USNS_spreading = {
		icon = GFX_decision_revolt
		allowed = { always = no }
		available = { hidden_trigger = { always = no } }
		is_good = no
		selectable_mission = no
		days_mission_timeout = RUS_USNS_speed
		fire_only_once = yes
		fixed_random_seed = no
		cancel_trigger = {
			202 = { NOT = { is_controlled_by = ROOT } } #Kyiv
		}

		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision cancel RUS_USNS_spreading"
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision timeout RUS_USNS_spreading"
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					any_neighbor_state = {
						NOT = {
							is_core_of = RUS
							state = 137 #Crimea
							#has_state_flag = RUS_USNS_removed
							compliance > 40
						}
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = RUS

		}

				FROM = { is_core_of = UKR }
			}
		}

			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision complete RUS_counter_insurgency"

				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_temp_CP_cost = RUS_USNS_cp_cost }

					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = -750
				}
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision remove RUS_counter_insurgency"
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_USNS_rebels } }
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_USNS_rebels }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_generic_rebels } }
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_generic_rebels }
				}
				set_state_flag = RUS_USNS_removed
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = { is_core_of = UKR }
						ROOT = { RUS_vladimir_manstein = { has_character_flag = RUS_UKR_governor } }
					}
					add_resistance = -50
				}
				else = {
					add_resistance = -25
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { is_core_of = UKR } }
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = RUS_USNS_spreading
					days = 15
				}
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

	RUS_operation_masuria = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_research
		allowed = { always = no }
		available = {
			64 = { is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_ally = yes } #Berlin
			GER = { exists = no }
		}
		cost = 50
		days_remove = 60
		fire_only_once = yes
		ai_will_do = { base = 100 }
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision remove RUS_operation_masuria"
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_tech = atomic_research
					NOT = { is_special_project_completed = sp:sp_nuclear_reactor }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { GER = { has_completed_focus = GER_nuclear_research } }
					sp:sp_nuclear_reactor = { add_project_progress_ratio = 0.2 }
				}
				else = {
					sp:sp_nuclear_reactor = { add_project_progress_ratio = 0.1 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { GER = { has_completed_focus = GER_nuclear_research } }
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = RUS_operation_masuria
					bonus = 0.5
					ahead_reduction = 1
					uses = 1
					category = nuclear
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = RUS_operation_masuria
					bonus = 0.25
					ahead_reduction = 1
					uses = 1
					category = nuclear
				}
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = RUS_operation_masuria
				bonus = 0.5
				uses = 1
				category = rocketry
				category = jet_technology
			}
		}

	}

	### The Road to War ###
	RUS_pressure_finland = {
		icon = GFX_decision_eng_trade_unions_demand

		allowed = { always = no }

		available = {
			threat > 0.35
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						OR = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
							is_guaranteed_by = GER
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_socialist_government = no }
					has_completed_focus = RUS_preemptive_war
				}
				else = {
					has_completed_focus = RUS_anti_capitalist_warfare
				}
			}
			can_declare_war_on = FROM
			NOT = { has_non_aggression_pact_with = FROM }
		}

		visible = {
			can_declare_war_on = FROM
			FROM = {
				owns_state = 146  #Karelia
				is_subject = no
				has_socialist_government = no
			}
			has_completed_focus = RUS_petrograd_security
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = RUS_preemptive_war }
				OR = {
					NOT = { can_declare_war_on = FROM }
					NOT = { 146 = { is_owned_by = FROM } } #Karelia
					has_non_aggression_pact_with = FROM
				}
			}
			else = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { can_declare_war_on = FROM }
					NOT = { 146 = { is_owned_by = FROM } } #Karelia
					has_non_aggression_pact_with = FROM
					FROM = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
					FROM = { is_guaranteed_by = GER }
				}
			}
		}

		targets = { FIN }
		target_root_trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = RUS_petrograd_security
		}
		target_trigger = {
			can_declare_war_on = FROM
			FROM = { owns_state = 146 } #Karelia
		}

		cost = 20
		days_remove = 21
		fire_only_once = yes
		war_with_target_on_remove = yes

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					RUS_dont_attack_if_vulnerable_or_preparing = yes
					FROM = { RUS_dont_attack_if_target_is_stronger = yes }
					FROM = { RUS_dont_attack_if_faction_is_stronger = yes }
					FROM = { RUS_dont_attack_if_overlord_is_stronger = yes }
				}
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = FIN_forpol option = FIN_FORPOL_NEUT } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FIN = { is_valid_peace_target = yes }
				OR = {
					AND = {
						FIN = { has_soclib_or_socdem_government = yes }
						RUS = {
							has_elected_government = yes
							is_monarchy = no
							NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = RUS_ivan_solonevich } }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						FIN = { has_completed_focus = FIN_mannerheims_ascendancy }
						RUS = {
							is_monarchy = yes
							RUS_ivan_solonevich = { is_second_in_command = no }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						FIN = { has_completed_focus = FIN_mannerheims_ascendancy }
						RUS = { has_country_flag = RUS_wrangel_ai }
					}
				}
				SCA_nordic_council_available = no
				var:141.owner = { has_socialist_government = no } # Stockholm
				NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_alliance_refused_@FROM }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = FIN_forpol option = FIN_FORPOL_NEUT } }
			}
		}

		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision cancel RUS_pressure_finland"
			clear_decision_attack_AI = yes
			add_political_power = 20
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision complete RUS_pressure_finland"
			setup_decision_attack_AI = yes
			set_country_flag = { flag = imminent_war days = 20 value = 1 }
			country_event = { id = russia_foreign_policy_events.30 days = 7 }
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision remove RUS_pressure_finland"
			clear_decision_attack_AI = yes
			if = {
				limit = { second_weltkrieg_has_begun = no }
				add_named_threat = {
					threat = 1
					name = RUS_aggression_threat_FROM
				}
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

				}
			}
		}

				factor = 0

					}

				}

	RUS_industrial_reparations = {
		icon = GFX_decision_hand_grab
		allowed = { always = no } #activated by effect

		visible = {
			any_owned_state = {
				free_building_slots = {
					size > 2
					building = industrial_complex
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				any_core_state = {
					industrial_complex > 2
					arms_factory > 2
					NOT = { has_state_flag = RUS_looted_state }
				}
			}
			num_of_owned_factories > 40
		}

		target_trigger = {
			num_of_owned_factories > 40
			FROM = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
		}

		cost = 80
		days_remove = RUS_ic_time_60

		ai_will_do = { factor = 100 }

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision complete RUS_industrial_reparations"
			FROM = {
				random_core_state = {
					limit = {
						industrial_complex > 2
						arms_factory > 2
						NOT = { has_state_flag = RUS_looted_state }
					}
					set_state_flag = RUS_looted_state
					remove_building = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
					}
					remove_building = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
					}
				}
				random_core_state = {
					limit = {
						industrial_complex > 2
						arms_factory > 2
						NOT = { has_state_flag = RUS_looted_state }
					}
					set_state_flag = RUS_looted_state
					remove_building = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
					}
					remove_building = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
					}
				}
				random_core_state = {
					limit = {
						industrial_complex > 2
						arms_factory > 2
						NOT = { has_state_flag = RUS_looted_state }
					}
					set_state_flag = RUS_looted_state
					remove_building = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
					}
					remove_building = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision remove RUS_industrial_reparations"
			random_core_state = {
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = arms_factory
						size > 2
					}
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			random_core_state = {
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = arms_factory
						size > 1
					}
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			random_core_state = {
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = industrial_complex
						size > 2
					}
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			random_core_state = {
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = industrial_complex
						size > 1
					}
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}
	FER_join_entente = {

							OR = {
								has_autonomy_state = union_republic

					}
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { country_exists = GER }
				has_war = no
			}
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					has_autonomy_state = union_republic
					has_autonomy_state = union_republic_autonomous
				}
				controls_all_owned_states = yes
			}
		}
		target_array = RUS_SSTR_tags
		target_root_trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = RUS_self_determination
		}
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				has_socialist_government = yes
			}
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 20
		ai_will_do = { factor = 100 }
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision complete RUS_add_to_union"
			FROM = { get_current_government_type = yes }
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = RUS_union_of_peoples } #Decentralised version
				set_autonomy = {
					target = FROM
					autonomy_state = union_republic_autonomous
					end_wars = no
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = FROM
					autonomy_state = union_republic
					end_wars = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = RUS_increased_devolution }
				FROM = { add_ideas = RUS_soc_economic_area }
			}
			hidden_effect = { FROM = { restore_previous_government_type = yes } }
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { tag = UKR }
					ROOT = { RUS_is_maximalist = yes }
				}
				UKR = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = totalist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = totalist
						long_name = UKR_totalistRUS_party_long
						name = UKR_totalistRUS_party
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = totalist
						popularity = 0.5
					}
					UKR_oleksandr_shumskyi = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								desc = UKR_oleksandr_shumskyi_leader_desc
								ideology = totalist_subtype
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { FROM = { is_in_faction_with = GER } }
				RUS_dont_attack_if_vulnerable_or_preparing = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = {
					tag = MON

						is_guaranteed_by = TIB

						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { RUS_dont_attack_if_target_is_stronger = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { RUS_dont_attack_if_faction_is_stronger = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { RUS_dont_attack_if_overlord_is_stronger = yes }
			}

				factor = 0
				FROM = {

					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = MON_fulfilling_the_dream_of_mongolian_independence
					}
				}
			}
		}

		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision cancel RUS_attack_soc"
			clear_decision_attack_AI = yes
			hidden_effect = { add_political_power = 10 }

				clr_country_flag = RUS_demanding_armenia

				limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = GER } }
				add_named_threat = {
					threat = 2
					name = RUS_aggression_threat_FROM
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = FROM
				type = annex_everything
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						original_tag = LAT

						is_in_faction = no
						is_subject = no
						is_ai = yes

					}

			}
			hidden_effect = {

					limit = { FROM = { tag = MON } }
					activate_mission = RUS_Socialist_defeat_mongolia
					MON = {
						add_ideas = RUS_mongolian_war_idea
						activate_mission = MON_hold_out_russian_war
					}
				}
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision complete RUS_favor_left"
			set_temp_variable = { RUS_relation_change = 2 }
			RUS_VST_left_relation = yes
			RUS_VST_centre_relation = yes
			if = {
				limit = { RUS_VST_centre = yes }
				set_temp_variable = { RUS_relation_change = -1 }
				RUS_VST_right_relation = yes
			}
			else = {
				set_temp_variable = { RUS_relation_change = -1 }
				RUS_SDS_relation = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_active_mission = RUS_left_ultimatum }
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = RUS_left_ultimatum
					days = 15
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { vst_left_var < 3 } } }
				set_country_flag = { flag = RUS_favor_left_cooldown value = 1 days = 150 }
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

RUS_sr_parliamentarian_decision_cat = {
	RUS_siberian_direction = {
		icon = GFX_decision_eng_trade_unions_support
		allowed = { always = no }
		is_good = no
		available = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				custom_override_tooltip = {
					tooltip = RUS_completed_3_siberia_decisions

				add_political_power = 75
				add_stability = -0.1
				set_temp_variable = { RUS_maximalist_influence_change = 6 }
				RUS_maximalist_influence = yes
				RUS_change_maximalist_influence_spirit = yes
				set_temp_variable = { RUS_maximalist_suspicion_change = 7 }
				RUS_maximalist_suspicion = yes
				add_to_variable = { RUS_disappear_political_opponents_var = 1 }
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

MIO_decisions = {
	### Mine Pilled decision unlocked through Dalzavod MIO
	RUS_dalzavod_mining_baltic_sea = {
		desc = RUS_dalzavod_mining_desc
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_naval_mine
		allowed = { always = no }
		available = {
			owns_state = 195
			has_war = yes
		}
		visible = {
			mio:RUS_dalzavod_organisation = {
				is_mio_trait_completed = dalzavod_upgrade_3
			}
		}

		custom_cost_text = CP_25
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			NOT = { command_power < 25 }
		}

		days_remove = 60

		ai_will_do = { base = 5 }
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision complete RUS_dalzavod_mining_baltic_sea"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = -25
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_mines = {
							region = 272
							amount = 900
						}
					}
				}
				add_mines = {
					region = 272
					amount = RUS_dalzavod_mines_number
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_mines = {
							region = 138
							amount = 900
						}
					}
				}
				add_mines = {
					region = 138
					amount = RUS_dalzavod_mines_number
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_mines = {
					region = 9
					amount = RUS_dalzavod_mines_number
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = RUS_dalzavod_total_mines_launched } }
				set_variable = { RUS_dalzavod_total_mines_launched = 0 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { RUS_dalzavod_total_mines_launched = RUS_dalzavod_mines_number }
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

	### TOZ Medal decision ###
	RUS_TOZ_Medals = {
		icon = GFX_decision_CHL_carabineros
		name = RUS_TOZ_Medals
		allowed = { always = no } #Activated by either traits toz_upgrade_2, toz_upgrade_4, toz_upgrade_1_2 or toz_upgrade_1_5
		available = { owns_state = 223 }

		priority = 50

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			mio:RUS_toz_organisation = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { funds < ROOT.TOZ_Required_Funds?500 } }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = RUS_TOZ_Funds_Medals_Requirement

		days_remove = 10

		ai_will_do = { base = 5 }
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision complete RUS_TOZ_Medals"
			hidden_effect = {
				set_temp_variable = { funds_change = TOZ_Required_Funds?500 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { funds_change = -1 }
				mio:RUS_toz_organisation = { add_mio_funds = var:funds_change }
			}
			RUS_TOZ_Hand_Out_Medals = yes
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}
	RUS_TOZ_Medals_automatic = {
		icon = GFX_decision_CHL_carabineros
		name = RUS_TOZ_Medals_automatic

		priority = 20

		allowed = { always = no } #Activated by either traits toz_upgrade_2, toz_upgrade_4, toz_upgrade_1_2 or toz_upgrade_1_5

		ai_will_do = { base = 0 }

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision complete RUS_TOZ_Medals_automatic"
			if = {
				limit = { has_active_mission = RUS_TOZ_Medals_automatic_mission }
				custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_TOZ_Medals_automatic_disable_tt
				hidden_effect = {
					remove_mission = RUS_TOZ_Medals_automatic_mission
					activate_targeted_decision = { target = FROM decision = RUS_TOZ_Medals_automatic }
					activate_targeted_decision = { target = FROM decision = RUS_TOZ_Medals }
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_TOZ_Medals_automatic_enable_tt
				hidden_effect = {
					remove_targeted_decision = { target = FROM decision = RUS_TOZ_Medals }
					activate_targeted_decision = { target = FROM decision = RUS_TOZ_Medals_automatic }
					activate_mission = RUS_TOZ_Medals_automatic_mission
				}
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}
	RUS_TOZ_Medals_automatic_mission = {
		icon = GFX_decision_CHL_carabineros
		name = RUS_TOZ_Medals_automatic_mission

		allowed = { always = no } #Activated by RUS_TOZ_Medals_automatic

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 10

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision timeout RUS_TOZ_Medals_automatic_mission"
			if = {
				limit = {
					mio:RUS_toz_organisation = {
						NOT = { check_variable = { funds < ROOT.TOZ_Required_Funds?500 } }
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { funds_change = TOZ_Required_Funds?500 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { funds_change = -1 }
				mio:RUS_toz_organisation = { add_mio_funds = var:funds_change }
				hidden_effect = { FROM = { activate_mission = RUS_TOZ_Medals_automatic_mission } }
				RUS_TOZ_Hand_Out_Medals = yes
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_TOZ_Medals_not_enough_funds
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}
	RUS_AV_Repeatable_Random_Funds = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_research
		name = RUS_AV_Repeatable_Random_Funds
		allowed = { always = no }

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			mio:RUS_av_organisation = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { funds < 250 } }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = RUS_AV_Funds_Requirement

		days_remove = 10

		ai_will_do = { base = 1000 }
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision complete RUS_AV_Repeatable_Random_Funds"
			mio:RUS_av_organisation = { RUS_AV_set_random_decaying_funds_bonus = yes }
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}
}
